rkai[cnb_max]=pow(kai[cnb_max],mod-2,mod)

    if y>x:
        return 0
    if x<0:return 0
    if y<0:return 0
    return (kai[x]*rkai[y]%mod)*rkai[x-y]%mod


def inv(n):
    return kai[n-1]*rkai[n]%mod

def solve():
    n = int(input())
    a = [*map(int, input().split())]
    b = a[:]
    for i in range((n - 1)):
        a[(i + 1)] += a[i]
    for i in range((n - 1), 0, (- 1)):
        b[(i - 1)] += b[i]
    (l, r) = (0, (n - 1))
    sol = 0
    while ((r - l) >= 1):
        if (a[l] == b[r]):
            sol = (((l + n) - r) + 1)
            l += 1
        if (a[l] < b[r]):
            l += 1
        else:
            r -= 1
    return sol
for _ in ([0] * int(input())):
    print(solve())

ans = None

    (acc, p) = (0, 0)
    for j in range((i - 1), (- 1), (- 1)):

        acc += (- x)
        p = (x * a[j])

def dfs(tree, i, h):
    if (i >= ((2 ** (h - 1)) - 1)):
        return [tree[i], 1]
    (ls, li) = dfs(tree, ((i * 2) + 1), h)
    (rs, ri) = dfs(tree, ((i * 2) + 2), h)
    res = (li * ri)
    if (ls != rs):
        res *= 2
    if (ls > rs):
        return [((tree[i] + rs) + ls), res]
    else:
        return [((tree[i] + ls) + rs), res]
